(the &#8220;Company&#8221;) announced the appointment of Staci L. Kroon to its Board of Directors (&#8220;Board&#8221;) effective immediately.</span></div><div><span><br/></span></div><div><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Ms. Kroon is President and Chief Executive Officer of BraunAbility, a global manufacturer of mobility vehicles and other mobility solutions, a position she has held since 2017.  Ms. Kroon also serves as a director of BraunAbility.  Before joining BraunAbility, Ms. Kroon spent 20 years at Eaton Corporation, a global power management company.</span></div><div><span><br/></span></div><div><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Ms. Kroon will be a Class III director and will serve on the Human Resources and Finance Committees. </span></div><div><span><br/></span></div><div><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Ms. Kroon will be compensated in accordance with the Company&#8217;s standard compensation policies and practices for the Board, the components of which were disclosed in the Company&#8217;s proxy statement for its 2022 annual meeting of shareholders filed with the Securities and Exchange Commission on October 31, 2022, in the section titled &#8220;Director Compensation,&#8221; provided that effective August 27, 2023, the value of the annual and new Board member equity retainer increased from $125,000 to $150,000.</span></div><div><span><br/></span></div><div><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">There are no transactions or relationships between the Company and Ms. Kroon that are reportable under Item 404(a) of Regulation S-K.</span></div><div><span><br/></span></div><div><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Ms. Kroon is expected to stand for election to the Board at the 2023 annual meeting of shareholders.</span></div><div><span><br/></span></div><div id="if60f1a52e726411ca0d8eec7a23aea7b_131"></div><div><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Item 7.01 Regulation FD Disclosure.</span></div><div><span><br/></span></div><div><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">On October 11, 2023, the Company issued a press release ann</span><span style="background-color:#ffffff;color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">ouncing the appointment of Ms. Kroon to the Board as described above under Item 5.02. A copy of the news release is furnished as Exhibit 99.1 and incorporated herein by reference.</span></div><div><span><br/></span></div><div id="if60f1a52e726411ca0d8eec7a23aea7b_10"></div><div She has also served as a board member and chairman for Nittan Global Tech. Kroon earned a bachelor&#8217;s degree in economics with a concentration in finance from the Wharton School of Business, a bachelor&#8217;s degree in mechanical engineering from the University of Pennsylvania and a postgraduate degree in design, manufacturing, and management from Cambridge University in England.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">&#8220;It is an honor to join the Winnebago Industries board of directors,&#8221; said Kroon. &#8220;This is an incredible opportunity to work alongside some of the most innovative minds in the industry and contribute to the strategic direction of a company that I deeply admire.
